<p>He is suing for his injuries, and she is suing for her injuries. This would therefore have two separate causes of action. However, the two causes of action would be in one plaint.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>When there is some common factual or legal basis among the various causes of action, they can be joined in one plaint.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="demand-for-relief">Demand for Relief<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#demand-for-relief" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Every plaint filed in an action contains a demand for relief from the court, often called a prayer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Courts have the power to two different types of relief, money damages and equitable relief.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Money damage usually means the award of money to the plaintiff as compensation for some loss.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Equitable relief, involves the court ordering the defendant to do something or to stop doing something.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Damages can be classified as:
(i) General damages;
(ii) Special damages;
(iii) Exemplary damages;
(iv) Aggravated damages;
(v) Punitive damages;
(vi) Nominal damages, etc.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The award and calculation of damages is a judicial function as opposed to a ministerial function.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>In the case of Kenya Revenue Authority v. Menginya Salim Murgini (2010) eKLR, the appellant appealed against the judgment of the trial court in an action for damages.</li>
</ul>
<p>The court awarded exemplary damages in the sum of KES 1 million but gave directions that the Deputy Registrar of the High Court "calculate" the other heads of damages which fact was the bone of contention in this appeal.</p>
<p>The court held that the court's delegation of the calculation of these heads of damages was erroneous since this amounted to converting a judicial function into a ministerial function.</p>
<p>Both the award and the level of quantum of damages were judicial functions which a court could not delegate to a deputy registrar.</p>
<p>A judgment must be complete and conclusive when pronounced in court.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="01">01<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#01" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>There are no hard and fast rules regarding damages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Having said that, most judicial decisions on damages are based on judicial precedents which set out rules on the maximum to be awarded or limit of damages that can be awarded on particular matters.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>However, a party must prove the damages incurred and, particularly, special damages must be specifically pleaded for a court to grant them.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The maximum awarded depends on the particular circumstance of the case and the prevailing market economy at the time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It is a question of fact.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The function of damages is to restore the prevailing party (plaintiff) to their original condition.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>This may not be possible, for example, where one has lost a limb.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Damages are therefore merely monetary compensation for the loss or injury suffered by the plaintiff.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="money-damages">Money damages<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#money-damages" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>These damages are known as compensatory damages as they compensate the plaintiffs for a loss they have sustained.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>They may be referred by other names depending on the kind of suit, for example in personal injury suits they may be known as special damages – out of pocket expense, e.g., doctors bills, loss of earnings, or general damages – pain and suffering, loss of use of a limb or disfigurement caused by a scar.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Sometimes the money damages would be in form of punitive or exemplary damages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>These are meant to punish the defendant and are awarded only when the defendant has committed some extremely offensive act or that it is in the public interest that such party be so punished as the breach of right affects society</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>In the course of the suit, the parties will inevitably incur substantial expenses, or costs.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>These can include filing fees, process server fees, deposition fees, and expert witness fees.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Costs are not included in compiling the plaintiff’s damages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If the plaintiff wins the lawsuit, he will generally be awarded certain costs in addition to the actual damages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>However, should the defendant win the case, he will be warded his costs from the plaintiff.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The issue of cost is however discretionary to the court</p>
</li>
<li></li>
<li>
<p>One element that is usually not included in the list of recoverable costs (unless the lawsuit is based on a contract that specifically provides for the payment thereof) are the advocate’s fees.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Parties are expected to pay their own advocate’s fees.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="collection-of-interest">Collection of Interest<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#collection-of-interest" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>A successful party to a case is entitled to collect interest accruing from the date of the suit to the date of the judgment and from the date of the judgment to the date of payment after judgment is entered.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Courts have the discretion to order interest to be paid on judgments for the period between the date when the cause of action arose and the date of the judgment, unless there is a special reason for not doing so.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>Under Section 26 (1) of the Civil Procedure Act (Cap. 21, Laws of Kenya), where a decree is for the payment of money, the courts may in the decree order interest at such rate as is deemed reasonable to be paid on the principal sum, adjudged from the date of the suit to the date of the decree, in addition to any interest adjudged on such principal sum for any period before the institution of the suit to the date of the decree, in addition to any interest adjudged on such principal sum for any period before the institution of the suit, with further interest at such rate as the court deems reasonable on the aggregate sum so adjudged from the date of the decree to the date of payment, or to such earlier date as the court thinks fit.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="non-monetary-relief">Non-monetary Relief<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#non-monetary-relief" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Circumstances under which non-monetary reliefs may be awarded include:</li>
<li>injunctions;</li>
<li>rescission; and</li>
<li>specific performance.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="equitable-relief">Equitable relief<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#equitable-relief" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Some legal disputes cannot be settled by an award of money damages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>For example, suppose Max sells Fred his business.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>As part of the sales agreement, Max agrees not to open a competing business within a 50km radius for a period of two years.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>However, two months after the sale, Max opens a competing business across the street from Fred.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>As a result, Fred’s business income substantially decreases. Although the money damages might compensate Fred for his past loss, if Max continues in business Fred will continue to lose money.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Fred would therefore prefer that the court order Max to close down his competing business.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Such an order would be known as equitable relief.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A plaint may combine a request for equitable relief and money damages.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Some of the more common types of equitable relief are:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Specific performance, rescission, restitution, declaratory relief, quiet title and injunction.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="provisional-remedies">Provisional remedies<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#provisional-remedies" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>In most courts, substantial time elapses between the filing of a plaint and the actual trial in that case.</li>
<li>When injunctive relief is the primary object of a suit, the plaintiff often requests some immediate provisional remedy from the court as soon as a plaint is filed.</li>
<li>Provisional remedies usually include a temporary restraining order, which usually compels the defendant to stop certain conduct immediately.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="01">01<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#01" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>This order will remain in effect for a very short time, usually until a hearing can be scheduled in court.</li>
<li>This hearing is for arguments from either side in support or against the TRO to remain in effect until the main trial or to be removed.</li>
<li>Should the court decide to keep the restraining order in effect, it will issue a preliminary injunction, an order remains in effect until the trial, at which time the injunction would become permanent if the plaintiff proves his case.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="injunctions">Injunctions<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#injunctions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>An injunction is an order of court restraining a person from doing a particular act.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It is a relief commonly issued in matters relating to breach of contract or liabilities in tort where damages would not be an adequate relief.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>There are different categories of injunctions including prohibitory and mandatory injunctions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Prohibitory injunctions act to restrain the defendant from doing certain things while mandatory injunctions require respondents to do certain things.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The purpose of these injunctions is: the preservation of property, legal rights and liabilities of parties until their conflicting claims are determined.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Before a party applies for an injunction, he or she must satisfy three conditions:
i. that it is a <em>prima facie</em> case with a high probability of success;
ii. that there is irreparable injury that cannot be compensated with damages; and
iii. that there is a balance of convenience in favour of the applicant.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="rescission">Rescission<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#rescission" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Where there is a breach of contract by one party the innocent party may choose to rescind the contract. If the aggrieved party intends to sue the guilty party for damages for breach of contract, he/she has to file a suit for rescission of the contract.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>When the court grants rescission, the aggrieved party is freed from all his/her obligations under the contract, and becomes entitled to compensation for any damage occasioned to him or her.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="specific-performance">Specific Performance<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#specific-performance" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>This is an equitable remedy.</li>
<li>It means the actual carrying out of the contract as agreed.</li>
<li>An aggrieved party may file a suit for specific performance, for a decree by the court directing the defendant to actually perform his/her obligation.</li>
<li>A decree for specific performance is granted only where it is just and equitable so to do, i.e where the legal remedy is inadequate or defective.</li>
<li>As a rule of law, specific performance is not granted where monetary compensation is an adequate relief or where the court cannot supervise the actual execution of the contract or where one of the parties to the agreement does not possess competency to contract and hence it cannot be granted for breach of contract.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="amendment-of-pleadings">Amendment of Pleadings<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#amendment-of-pleadings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>A party can seek to amend pleadings at any time before the close of pleadings, and thereafter with the leave of court.</li>
<li>Under Order 5, Rule 5 of the Civil Procedure Rules, the court may either on its own motion or on the application of any party order any document to be amended in such a manner as it directs.</li>
</ul>
<p>This is done so as to determine the real question in controversy between the parties and to correct any defect or error in the proceedings.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Rules relating to the amendment of pleadings lie within the context of the principle that ‘one is bound by one's own pleadings’.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If one is to be bound by one's pleadings, then one should be allowed to amend them whenever necessity arises and subject to the rules relating to such amendments.</p>
</li>
<li></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>In the case of Michael Richardson v. Rand Blair Trading as Momentum Feeds and Another [2012] UG Comm C 39 the High Court of Uganda held that one of the principles is that amendments should be freely allowed unless it is done mala fide and/or occasions prejudice or injustice to the other party which cannot be compensated by award of costs.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="procedure-for-applying-for-leave-to-amend">Procedure for applying for leave to amend<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#procedure-for-applying-for-leave-to-amend" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>In the event a party wants to amend the claim, leave of court must be sought.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>This is provided for in Order 5, Rule 3 of the Civil Procedure Rules, which states that a party should make an application to court for leave to amend the plaint at any stage of the proceedings and it shall be granted as the court thinks just to do so.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Application for leave to amend is made by way of Chamber Summons and in most cases you can make an oral application in court but it is always safer to follow the oral application with a written one.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Note however, a party may undertake to amend their pleadings at any time throughout trial as long as consent is sought and obtained from the other party.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cases">Cases<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cases" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Justus Kyalo Mutunga v. Labh Singh Harnam[2012]eKLR</li>
<li>Gachui Akothae Rengerua v Zena Salim Ahmed(Suing as the administratrix of the estate of Salim Ahemed Salem)[2012] eKLR</li>
</ul>
<p>LESSON 10</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="issue-and-service-of-summons">ISSUE AND SERVICE OF SUMMONS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#issue-and-service-of-summons" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="issue-of-summons-0-5-r-1">Issue of Summons 0.5 r.1<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#issue-of-summons-0-5-r-1" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Upon filing the suit summons shall issue to the defendant to appear and answer in court</li>
<li>The summons shall be prepared by the plaintiff or their advocate and filed with a copy of the plaint</li>
<li>The summons shall be signed and sealed with the seal of the court by a judge or an officer designated by them within 30 days from date of filing</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Cognisance shall be had of the defendant’s place of residence to allow them to make an appearance. However, the period shall not be less than 10 days</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The summons shall be collected for service within 30 days of issue or of notice of issue</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="duration-and-renewal-of-summons-r-2">Duration and renewal of summons r.2<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#duration-and-renewal-of-summons-r-2" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Summons shall be valid initially for 12 months from the date of issue</li>
<li>A concurrent summon shall be valid initially for the period of validity of the original summons as long as they have not expired by the time the concurrent summons are issued</li>
</ul>
<p>Where the summons have not been served on the defendant, the court may extend the validity of such summons from time to time if it deems just to do so</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>An application for extension of validity of summons shall be made by filing an affidavit of service indicating how many attempts have been made at service and their results</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>An order may be made without advocate or plaintiff being heard</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If no application is made for extension of validity of summons, the court may without notice dismiss the suit upon expiry of 24 months from date of issue of original summons</p>
</li>
<li></li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="enlargement-of-time">Enlargement of time<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#enlargement-of-time" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>So what would happen if an extension of the validity of summons was sought after the expiry of the requisite 12 or 24 months?</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="0-50-r-6">0.50 r.6<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#0-50-r-6" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Where a limited time has been fixed for doing any act or taking any proceedings under these Rules, or by summary notice or by order of the court, the court shall have power to enlarge such time upon such terms (if any) as the justice of the case may require, and such enlargement may be ordered although the application for the same is not made until after the expiration of the time appointed or allowed</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>The court therefore has discretionary jurisdiction to enlarge the time for filing an application seeking the extension of validity of expired summons</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>However, it is accepted in practice that a court should not exercise its discretion to enlarge time, where the claim should be barred by the limitation of statutes in absence of the enlargement in time. Doyle v Kaufman (1887) 3 QBD 7</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="delivery-or-transmission-of-summons-for-service-r-5">Delivery or transmission of summons for service r.5<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#delivery-or-transmission-of-summons-for-service-r-5" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Once the summons have been issued by the court to the defendant the summons will be delivered for service –</li>
<li>a) to any person authorized by the court</li>
<li>b) to an advocate, or advocate’s clerk approved by court</li>
<li>c) To any subordinate court having jurisdiction in the place defendant resides</li>
<li>d) To an officer appointed by the Police Act or AP Act</li>
<li>e) To a licensed courier service provider approved by court</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="mode-of-service-r-6-7-8-11">Mode of service r.6,7,8,11<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mode-of-service-r-6-7-8-11" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Service of summons shall be by tendering or delivering a duplicate of the summons and the recipient signs an acknowledgement on the original – this rule is mandatory and non-compliance means service has not been effected</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where there are many defendants, service shall be made on each defendant</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where practicable, service shall be made on defendant in person, unless he has an agent authorized to accept service – for. e.g. Advocate with instructions to accept service and enter appearance – judgement in default of appearance may be entered after this service</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Service of summons could be effected on an adult residing with the person sued, or an agent duly empowered</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If the service is not effected on the defendant personally, and the wife is served but refuses to sign, this service is not effective</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Neither is service upon a wife of a defendant who is known to have travelled abroad effective</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="time-of-service">Time of service<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#time-of-service" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Service of summons and court processes must comply with the time and day of the service</li>
<li>Therefore service on Sundays and public holidays is prohibited</li>
<li>Is this restrictive nature of this Order to be desired, in reference to the realities in Kenya?</li>
<li>Remember, the rationale for issuance of summonses and notices is to notify the other party about the pending suit in court!</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="affidavit-of-service-r-15">Affidavit of Service r.15<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#affidavit-of-service-r-15" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The serving officer in all cases in which summons has been served shall swear and annex to the original summons an affidavit of service stating the time when and the manner in which summons was served and the name and address of the person served and witnessing the delivery of summons.</li>
<li>Failure to record the name and address of the person identifying the person to be served renders the affidavit of service incurably defective</li>
<li>The affidavit of service shall be in Form No 4 of Appendix A.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="where-defendant-refuses-service-or-cannot-be-found">Where defendant refuses service or cannot be found<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#where-defendant-refuses-service-or-cannot-be-found" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>r.14</p>
<ul>
<li>Where the serving officer, after using all due and reasonable diligence, cannot find the defendant, or any person on whom service can be made, the serving officer and or advocate seized with the matter shall apply for substituted service.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="substituted-service">Substituted service<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#substituted-service" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Where the court is satisfied that for any reason the summons cannot be served as under the rules of this Order, the court may on application order the summons -</li>
<li>to be served by affixing a copy thereof in some conspicuous place in the court-house,</li>
<li>and also upon some conspicuous part of the house, if any, in which the defendant is known to have last resided or carried on business or personally worked for gain</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The person effecting the service shall then return the original to the court from which it was issued, together with an affidavit of service.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Instead of going through the grief of having to extend summons, one should consider the option of simply applying through Order 5, rule 17(4) for substituted service by advertisement as under Form 5 Appendix A</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The procedure need not be expensive as the full title of the court case need not be included</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Use the following format:
SUBSTITUTED SERVICE BY ADVERTISEMENT
(O. 5 r. 17)</p>
<p>To Jameson Walker</p>
<p>P. O. Box 53, 00700 Nairobi</p>
<p>Take notice that a plaint has been filed in the Milimani High Court at Nairobi in civil suit no. 1234 of 2014 in which you are named as the defendant. Service of summons to you has been ordered by means of this advertisement. A copy of the summons and plaint may be obtained at the court at P. O. Box 48010-00100 Nairobi.</p>
<p>And further take notice that unless you enter an appearance within 21 days the case will be heard in your absence.</p>
<p>GM Advocates</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="service-on-corporation-r-3">Service on corporation r.3<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#service-on-corporation-r-3" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Service on corporations should be served on the secretary, director or principal officer of the corporation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If the process server is unable to get hold of any officers of the company he can undertake service by:</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>a) leaving it at the registered office of the corporation</p>
<p>b) by sending it by prepaid registered post or by a licensed courier service provider approved by the court to the registered postal address of the corporation, or</p>
<p>c) by leaving it at the place where the corporation carries on business, or</p>
<p>d) by sending it by registered post to the last known postal address of the corporation</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="mode-of-service-on-government">Mode of service on government<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mode-of-service-on-government" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="r-9">r.9<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#r-9" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>Service on the government shall be effected by leaving the document at the office of the AG or their designated agent or a person belonging to that office</li>
<li>By posting it in a prepaid registered envelope addressed to AG or designated agent</li>
<li>For purpose of the Rules, documents served on government in connection with civil proceedings shall not require personal service</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="service-out-of-kenya-r-21">Service out of Kenya r.21<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#service-out-of-kenya-r-21" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>This will be allowed by the court where:</li>
<li>The subject-matter of the suit is immovable property situate in Kenya</li>
<li>Where any act, deed, will or contract involving immovable property situate in Kenya needs to be construed, rectified, set aside or enforced in the suit</li>
<li>Any relief is sought against a person domiciled or ordinarily resident in Kenya</li>
</ul>
<p>The suit is for settlement of the estate of a deceased whom at the time of his death was domiciled in Kenya, or for the execution of trusts where the person to be served is a trustee and it is executed according to Kenyan law</p>
<p>o Where the suit is in respect to a contract which is:</p>
<p>a) made in Kenya</p>
<p>b) made by or through an agent residing or trading in Kenya, on behalf of a principal trading or residing outside Kenya</p>
<p>c) governed by the Laws of Kenya</p>
<p>d) which provides that the courts of Kenya have jurisdiction to hear and determine suit on the contract</p>
<p>0 Suit is founded on a tort committed in Kenya</p>
<p>0 An injunction is sought to be done in Kenya, a nuisance to be prevented in Kenya with or without damages being sought</p>
<p>0 Where a person residing out of Kenya is a necessary party to a suit brought against a party served in Kenya</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="application-for-leave-to-serve-out-of-kenya-r-25">Application for leave to serve out of Kenya r.25<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#application-for-leave-to-serve-out-of-kenya-r-25" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The plaint must state the facts on which court is asked to assume jurisdiction</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Application by way of a Request for Service Abroad, Form No. 8 Appendix A indicating therein that applicant undertakes to be responsible for all expenses incurred in respect of this service</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>to be supported by an affidavit or evidence, stating that the deponent believes that the plaintiff has a good cause of action</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It should also state in what place the defendant is or will probably be found</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Or whether the person is a Commonwealth citizen or a British protected person or not</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>And the grounds on which the application is made</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Any failure to make full and fair disclosure may justify discharging an order for service out of jurisdiction</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If it appears to the court that the case is a proper one to serve out of Kenya, the application shall be granted.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The high court shall issues sealed summons through the Registrar.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="service-out-of-kenya">Service out of Kenya<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#service-out-of-kenya" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Where the person is a Commonwealth citizen, a Letter Forwarding Request for Service Abroad as under Form No. 7 Appendix A from the CJ</li>
<li>shall be addressed to the Cabinet Secretary in charge of Foreign Affairs for transmission of the summons to the defendant, in that country,</li>
<li>and also requesting evidence of service to be certified to the High Court or declared upon oath as would be undertaken in the Commonwealth Jurisdiction to prove service of legal process</li>
</ul>
<p>A notice of summons shall be served upon a person who is not a Commonwealth citizen and shall be as in Form No. 6, Appendix A, r.28</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Letter Forwarding Request for Service Abroad as under Form No. 7 Appendix A from the CJ shall accompany the notice of summons</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>shall be addressed to the Cabinet Secretary in charge of Foreign Affairs for transmission of the notice of summons to the defendant, in that country,</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>and also requesting evidence of service to be certified to the High Court or declared upon oath or in a manner consistent with usage or practice of the courts where defendant is served, to prove service of legal process</p>
</li>
<li></li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="r-29">r.29<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#r-29" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The notice shall be sealed with the seal of the High Court of Kenya</li>
<li>and shall be forwarded by the Registrar to the Cabinet Secretary in charge of Foreign Affairs</li>
<li>together with a copy translated in the language of the country in which service is to be effected with a request for further transmission of the notice through the diplomatic channel to the Government of the country in which leave to serve notice of summons has been effected;</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="substituted-service-abroad">Substituted Service Abroad<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#substituted-service-abroad" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>r.29</p>
<ul>
<li>If the official certificate or declaration upon oath declares that efforts to serve notice of summons have been without effect,</li>
<li>the Registrar shall issue a Certificate of Service of Foreign Process as under Form 11 Appendix A,</li>
<li>attaching thereto, the original request for service of process, the process received, and evidence of service</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>
<p>through an ex parte application by the plaintiff, accompanied by all the above, the court may order for substituted service of notice by and Order to Bespeak Request for Substituted Service Abroad as under Form 9 Appendix A</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>the order shall be accompanied by Letter Forwarding Request for Substituted Service Form No. 10 Appendix A, from the CJ.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>and, a Certificate for Service of Foreign Process shall then be filed in the High Court.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="cases">Cases<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#cases" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Justus Nyaribo v Clerk to Nyamira County Assembly [2013] eKLR Petition Case No. 2 of 2013 (it would be an absurdity if a person duly appears in court and then seeks an order declaring that the summons has not been duly served on them)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Rose Florence Wanjiru v Standard Chartered Bank of Kenya Limited &amp; 2 others [2014] eKLR</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>LESSON 11: WRITTEN STATEMENT OF DEFENCE</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="responding-to-pleadings">RESPONDING TO PLEADINGS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#responding-to-pleadings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="memorandum-of-appearance">Memorandum of Appearance<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#memorandum-of-appearance" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The defendant shall within the time stipulated in the summons enter an appearance as under Form No. 12 of Appendix A (O.6 r2(1))</li>
<li>The memorandum shall contain the name of the defendant (as appearing in the summons), the date (of entering appearance) and the signature of the person so summoned or their advocate.</li>
<li>Also include the address for service and the postal address (if different).</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="01">01<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#01" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Where the defendant is a firm, the appearance must list the individual partners by name with the description “Partners in the firm of”.</li>
<li>Where the defendant is an individual trading in a name other than his own, he must appear in his own name with the addition of the description “trading as”.</li>
<li>Where the defendant is a corporation the appearance must be either by an advocate or by an officer of the corporation duly authorized so to do under the corporate seal.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="written-statement-of-defence">Written Statement of Defence<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#written-statement-of-defence" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The written statement of the defence is a pleading presented by the defendant intended to reply to the allegations on the plain.</p>
<ul>
<li>Where a defendant has been served with a summons to appear:</li>
<li>a) they shall enter appearance in the court;</li>
<li>b) file their defence within 14 days after they have entered an appearance in the suit;</li>
<li>c) serve it on the plaintiff within 14 days from the date of filing the defence; and</li>
<li>d) file an affidavit of service (O7 r1)</li>
</ul>
<p>The plaintiff shall thereafter enter their reply to the defence within 14 days from service of the defence (O7, r17(1))</p>
<ul>
<li>All pleadings subsequent to the plaint shall be filed in duplicate (O7, r18(1))</li>
<li>The duplicate shall be returned to the party to serve to the address of service of the opposing parties within 7 days, or the court can do this itself should that opposing party attend at the registry before delivery (O7, r18(2,3))</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="contents-of-defence-or-counter-claim">Contents of Defence or Counter Claim<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#contents-of-defence-or-counter-claim" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The defence or counterclaim shall be accompanied by:</li>
<li>a) an affidavit as under O4 r1(2), where there is a counter claim;</li>
<li>b) a list of witnesses to be called at trial;</li>
<li>c) written statements signed by witnesses, except expert witness; and</li>
<li>d) copies of documents to be relied on at trial (O7, r5)</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="functions-of-a-wsd">Functions of a WSD<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#functions-of-a-wsd" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>The function of a WSD is to state the grounds and the material facts on which the defendant relies for their defence.</li>
<li>The WSD is to inform the plaintiff precisely how much of the statement of the claim the defendant relies on to defeat the claim of the plaintiff.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="matters-specifically-pleaded">Matters specifically pleaded<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#matters-specifically-pleaded" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The defendant may also specifically plead any matter, for e.g., release, inevitable accident, act of God, any relevant statute of limitation, or any fact showing illegality —</p>
<p>(a) which they alleges may make the claim not maintainable;</p>
<p>(b) which if not specifically pleaded, will take the other party by surprise; or</p>
<p>(c) which raises a fact not arising from the previous pleading (O2 r4(1))</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="how-may-an-opposing-party-respond-to-pleadings">How may an opposing party respond to pleadings<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#how-may-an-opposing-party-respond-to-pleadings" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>In response the defendant has the following options, they may:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>request further and better particulars;</li>
<li>admit the facts stated but raise a question of law as to their legal effect;</li>
<li>deny or refuse to admit the facts;</li>
<li>confess or admit the facts and avoid their effect by asserting fresh facts which afford an answer to them;</li>
<li>admit or make an admission;</li>
<li>plead a counterclaim; or</li>
<li>state facts that give rise to a set-off.</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="1-seeking-further-particulars">1. Seeking further particulars<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#1-seeking-further-particulars" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>Seeking further particulars summons, and before the expiry of the time within which to respond, defendant may by notice in writing to the plaintiff, request for further information as under Request for Particulars Form No. 2 Appendix A (O2 r1(2))</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The plaintiff may provide further particulars as under Form No. 3 Appendix A (O2 r10(6))</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Once this notice has been given, appearance should be made within 4 days from the defendant’s notice in writing acknowledging that they are satisfied; or</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>within 4 days after the court decides no further information is required, upon application of plaintiff by chamber summons served not less than 7 days before return day (O2 r1(3))</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It is an indirect way of attacking the plaintiffs suit because failure to provide may lead to an application to strike out pleadings for want of information. (O2 r1(2))</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Replying to a pleading in such a way as to inquire for further particulars may force your opponent to amend.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="2-raising-a-point-of-law">2. Raising a point of law<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#2-raising-a-point-of-law" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>The defendant may raise a point of law (O2 r9)</li>
<li>The distinction between pleading the law, which is not permitted, and raising a point of law which is permitted, is that by pleading the law a party would in effect be pleading conclusions of law, which could obscure the facts of the case.</li>
<li>On the other hand, by raising a point of law, a party would help define or identify or isolate an issue or question of law on the facts pleaded</li>
</ul>
<p>It is advisable to file a formal notice of objection on a point of law, file it and serve it on the opponent, this is meant to notify them on the point of law you intend to raise</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>….‘Take notice that the defendant intends to raise an objection on a point of law’</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where matters touch on jurisdiction they must be heard as a preliminary matter before anything else</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Objections could be validity of a custom, questions of jurisdiction of a court, whether a conversation was privileged, etc.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Raising an objection on a point of law is a preliminary issue and where sustained it should have the effect of having the suit struck out or dismissed at that point.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="how-to-raise-a-point-of-law">How to raise a point of law<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#how-to-raise-a-point-of-law" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>An objection in a point of law may be pleaded together with any number of traverses and special pleas.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Each objection should however:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>(a) be stated in a separate paragraph following those which deal with the facts;</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>(b) raise a point of substance, not merely a technicality, an objection to some defect of form; and</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>(c) state succinctly the ground for the objection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Any point of law, which requires serious prolonged argument, should ordinarily be raised in pleading and dealt with, if appropriate, as a preliminary issue</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>An objection in point of law must be taken clearly and explicitly, and the points precisely defined</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where all the allegations in the plaint are admitted but an objection in a point of law is raised in the defence, no evidence will be admitted at the trial since there is no issue of fact on the pleadings</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The party may raise a point of law in trial</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Parties are not entitled by their pleadings to raise abstract or hypothetical questions of law</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="3-traverse-or-deny">3. Traverse or Deny<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#3-traverse-or-deny" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>A traverse in defence is a denial of an allegation of fact made in the plaint</li>
<li>What does it do:</li>
<li>(a) It negates such allegation</li>
<li>(b) It operates to contradict what is alleged and to put it in issue</li>
<li>(c) It casts upon the plaintiff the burden of proving the allegations denied</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="general-rule">General Rule<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#general-rule" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Any allegation of fact made by a party in his pleading shall be deemed admitted by the opposing party unless it is traversed in opposing party's pleadings (O2 r11(1))</li>
<li>A traverse may be made by a denial or a statement of non-admission, expressly or by implication (O2 r11(2))</li>
<li>The party traversing the alleged fact must do so specifically with reference to the alleged fact, in their pleadings (O2 r11(3))</li>
<li>However, an allegation that a party has suffered damage and any allegation as to the amount of damages shall be deemed traversed unless specifically admitted (O2 r11(4))</li>
</ul>
<p>A traverse must not be vague or general or evasive. Rather it must be specific and must deal with each allegation of fact and as regards each must answer the point of substance</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>A defendant must deal specifically with every allegation of fact made by the plaintiff. He must clearly admit or deny it. Any half admission or half denial is evasive</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Any ambiguous phrase will be construed into an admission of it</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>It will also look weak to deny everything in your opponent’s pleadings – it suggests that you have no substantial defence to it</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>As a rule, a general denial is not admissible, however, it is acceptable where there is already a specific denial</p>
</li>
<li></li>
<li>
<p>Omnibus denial:</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>...save as hereinafter expressly admitted the defendant denies each and every allegation contained in the plaint as if the same were set forth verbatim and traversed seriatim</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="4-confession-and-avoidance">4. Confession and Avoidance<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-confession-and-avoidance" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Where the defendant decides to confess and avoid, this means that he admits the allegations subject to some facts, which adversely affect the claim.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The technique of confession and avoidance is used where the defendant admits the existence of some allegations but avoids the legal consequences of the existence of those facts from which the allegations emanate</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Eg., in a suit of wrongful dismissal
“the defendant denies that he wrongfully
dismissed the plaintiff from the
employment”</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>It comes out clearly that the Defendant admits he dismissed the plaintiff but not wrongfully.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="5-admission">5. Admission<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#5-admission" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Admission may be express or implied by the non-traverse of a material fact in the plaint</li>
<li>Defendant ought to admit material facts which have no controversy – he should admit any facts in which it is not in his interest to disprove or he does not have the power to disprove</li>
<li>An express admission ought to be clear, bold and unambiguous and should specify precisely what it is that is being admitted</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="6-counter-claim-07-r3">6. Counter-claim 07 r3<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#6-counter-claim-07-r3" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>A defendant may reply to the plaint by way of counter-claim</li>
<li>In this cross-suit they will be required to divide their written statement of defence into two sections:</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>The defence</li>
<li>A statement of claim against the plaintiff</li>
</ol>
<ul>
<li>The counter claim must be specifically pleaded(07, r7)</li>
</ul>
<p>THE REPUBLIC OF KENYA
IN THE HIGH COURT AT KISII
CIVIL SUIT NO. 16 OF 2016</p>
<p>BLUE SKY MOON INC...PLAINTIFF
V
HAWK MI SIDE...DEFENDANT
WRITTEN STATEMENT OF DEFENCE AND
COUNTER CLAIM</p>
<p>Even though the plaintiff was the first person to commence the litigation, it may happen that the defendant also has some claim against the plaintiff</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Usually the option is that the defendant will have a choice either to institute a separate suit or set up their claim in the defence</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If the court finds that the defendant’s claim can be determined within the same suit without delay, inconvenience or prejudice to justice, then the court will allow it</p>
</li>
<li></li>
</ul>
<p>E.g., Suppose the bank sues you over a debt, the bank will be the plaintiff over you. Suppose the Bank overcharged in calculations? You can counterclaim on the overcharging</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Where a party, not a party to the suit, is included in a counter claim they shall be summoned to appear by being served with a copy of the defence as under the rules of service of summons (O7, r9)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The party shall enter an appearance and file a reply to such defence within 15 days from service of copy of counter claim and serve all parties to the suit (O7, r11)</p>
</li>
<li></li>
<li>
<p>Where a suit by the plaintiff is stayed, discontinued or dismissed the court may nonetheless proceed with the counter claim (O7, r13)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The plaintiff shall enter their defence to counter claim in the same way as a defendant enters their defence (O7, r17(3))</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="7-set-off">7. Set off<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#7-set-off" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>Two types of set off:</li>
<li>Legal set off</li>
<li>Equitable set off</li>
<li>Legal set off exists when there is a liquidated sum of money; the plaintiff must owe the defendant the liquidated sum of money</li>
<li>An equitable set off arises where there is no liquidated amount and the suit is settled by adjudication</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="counter-claim-set-off">Counter-claim &amp; Set off<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#counter-claim-set-off" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>There are two major distinctions</li>
</ul>
<ol>
<li>
<p>a setoff is in the nature of a defence ("shield"), whereas a counter-claim is in the nature of a cross-action ("sword").
If the plaintiff obtains judgment or the action is stayed or dismissed, the setoff also comes to an end whereas in such events a counter-claim may still be proceeded with.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Under a setoff, the defendant can recover nothing against the plaintiff for they can only use the setoff as a defence or answer to plaintiff's claim equal to the amount of the setoff. A plaintiff cannot therefore obtain a security of costs in respect of a setoff</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A setoff may be raised only in respect of a claim by the plaintiff of a sum of money, whether such sum be a claim for debt or damages</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A setoff can only be used by way of defence to the plaintiffs action. Therefore it can be used “as a shield and not a sword”</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="consequences-of-non-appearance">CONSEQUENCES OF NON-APPEARANCE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#consequences-of-non-appearance" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>LECTURE 11A: DEFAULT OF DEFENCE AND FAILURE TO SERVE</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Where no appearance has been entered for a minor or a person of unsound mind, before proceeding further the plaintiff shall make an application to the court for an order for a guardian for the defendant to appear and defend the suit (O10,r1)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where the defendant fails to appear, the plaintiff shall file an affidavit of service of summons (O10,r2)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If the claim is for a liquidated amount and the defendant fails to make an appearance by the date fixed by the summons a request shall be made to the court by a Request for Judgment as per Form no. 13 Appendix A</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The court shall enter judgment for a sum not exceeding the liquidated sum claimed, together with interest from the date filed to the date of judgment and costs, at reasonable rate as per the court (O10,r4(1))</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where the claim is for liquidated sum and other claim, the awarding of costs shall be determined after the other claim has been settled (O10, r4(2))</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where the plaint makes a liquidated demand with any other claim and there are several defendants, some of whom fail to appear as required, the court shall, on request as per Form 13 of Appendix A, enter judgment against any defendant failing to appear as according to (O10, r4)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Execution may ensue upon such judgment and decree, against those failing to appear</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Notwithstanding the above, the plaintiff may still proceed with their action against those who have appeared (O10, r5)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where the plaint filed for pecuniary damages or for detention of goods with or without damages and the defendant fails to appear, upon an application by the plaintiff for a request for judgment the court may enter an interlocutory judgment against defendant</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>In the Request for Judgment the plaintiff will delete the component for request for costs</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Plaintiff shall then set down the suit for assessment of the damages or value of goods and damages (O10, r6)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where the plaint is for pecuniary damages or for detention of goods with or without damages and there are several defendants, and some appear and some fail to appear, the court shall upon request in Form 13 Appendix A, enter interlocutory judgment upon those failing to appear</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Damages or value of goods and damages shall be assessed at the time of the hearing of those defendants who have appeared (O10, r7)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="liquidated-unliquidated-demand">Liquidated/Unliquidated Demand<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#liquidated-unliquidated-demand" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>A liquidated demand must be capable of calculation.</li>
<li>A liquidated demand is a claim for a specific sum of money.</li>
<li>If the demand is for any amount which has not already been calculated but is merely a matter of arithmetic, the demand is also a liquidated demand.</li>
<li>A claim for unliquidated damage is not a liquidated demand because the quantum of the claim requires judicial assessment beyond arithmetic calculation.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="procedure">PROCEDURE<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#procedure" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Requests for ex-parte judgments are made where memorandum to enter appearance and defense have not been filed within the prescribed time.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>File is retrieved, court fees paid and file marked to deputy registrar for perusal and directions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Final or interlocutory judgment is entered by the deputy registrar depending on the reliefs sought in the plaint.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Matter is set down for formal proof hearing upon entry of interlocutory judgment.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A request for entry of judgment is accompanied by an affidavit stating mode of service by the advocate’s court process server annexing a copy of license to serve.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Attempts to file memorandum of appearance as per Form No. 12 Appendix A, and or defense after directions to enter judgment or entry of judgment are placed before the deputy registrar for directions.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>All requests for judgment and entry of judgment shall be serialized.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Where the defendant is the government, a formal application for leave to enter judgment against the government must be made.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>No judgment in default of appearance or pleading may be entered against the government without leave of the court</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Application for leave to be served not less than 7 days before its return (O10, r8)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Subject to O10 r4, the general rule for all other suits not specifically provided for by O.10 is that the plaintiff may set down the matter for hearing, where there is non-appearance by party served (O10, r9)</p>
</li>
<li>
